Every other feature index.ts and every hooks/index.ts is dead — routes import concrete paths e.g. app/routes/history.tsx:1 `@/features/history/components/page`, app/routes/review.tsx:1, providers.tsx:1. components/shared/index.ts has ZERO consumers (all 7 imports go to concrete files e.g. features/onboarding/components/steps/api-key-step.tsx:5). components/ui/severity/index.ts is bypassed by history-insights-pane.tsx:7 (concrete) yet used by analysis-summary.tsx:6 (barrel) — inconsistent. components/layout/index.ts and testing/index.ts are consumed mostly by tests. app/providers/index.tsx is NOT a barrel (it defines the AppProviders component) and must be kept.
Fix: Delete every listed index.ts. Rewrite the few remaining barrel imports to concrete files: app/routes/onboarding.tsx -> `@/features/onboarding/components/onboarding-wizard`; __root.tsx + the test files importing `@/components/layout` -> `@/components/layout/global-layout` / `./footer`; analysis-summary.tsx -> `@/components/ui/severity/severity-breakdown`; all `@/testing` imports -> the concrete render/factories/utils files; review-progress-view.tsx -> `@/components/ui/progress/progress-list`. Keep app/providers/index.tsx (real composition module).
round: 1

### F-002 · high · tests · apps/web/src/hooks/use-action-row-navigation.test.tsx:1-233, libs/keys/src/hooks/use-action-row-navigation.test.tsx:110-337, libs/keys/src/hooks/use-action-row-navigation.ts:1

The test renders a test-only fixture 'TestFooterNavigation' (no real web component) and re-asserts the keys hook's contract: web cases map 1:1 to libs/keys cases. test-behavior-not-implementation skill: 'Don't test what the framework/library already tests' and 'Redundant tests are worse than no tests.' This is upstream library behavior re-tested through a synthetic fixture, not a web adoption seam.
Fix: Delete apps/web/src/hooks/use-action-row-navigation.test.tsx (and its orphaned synthetic fixture). The contract is fully covered by libs/keys/src/hooks/use-action-row-navigation.test.tsx. If a genuine web-integration assertion is wanted, it belongs in the test of an actual web component that consumes the hook (e.g. no-changes-view.tsx / api-key-missing-view.tsx), not a standalone re-test of the keys API.
round: 1

### F-003 · high · architecture · apps/docs/vite.config.ts:77-135, apps/docs/src/layouts/header.tsx:1, apps/docs/src/components/docs-mdx/blocks/source-viewer-block.tsx:3-15, apps/docs/src/features/theme/components/preview-panel.tsx, libs/ui/package.json

Fix: Per D5: delete apps/docs/registry/ and its registry/tsconfig.json; remove the registry alias block in vite.config.ts (lines 79-132) and the `./registry/tsconfig.json` entry in the viteTsConfigPaths projects list (line 25); rewrite the ~40 src imports `@/components/ui/<c>/<c>` -> `@diffgazer/ui/components/<c>` and `@/hooks/use-<h>` -> `@diffgazer/ui/hooks/<h>` (codemod with ts-morph). Keep the lockstep gates (prepare:artifacts + validate:artifacts:check).
round: 1

### F-004 · high · naming · apps/landing/src/App.tsx:1, apps/landing/src/App.test.tsx:5, apps/landing/src/main.tsx:3
apps/landing App.tsx / App.test.tsx are the only PascalCase source filenames in the repo
Evidence: D1 mandates kebab-case files everywhere, PascalCase only for the exported symbol. A repo-wide scan returns exactly one hit: apps/landing/src/App.tsx. The file exports `function App()` and is imported as `./App` by main.tsx:3 and App.test.tsx:5. Case-only-distinct filenames are also fragile on case-insensitive filesystems.
Fix: Rename apps/landing/src/App.tsx -> apps/landing/src/app.tsx and apps/landing/src/App.test.tsx -> apps/landing/src/app.test.tsx. Keep the exported symbol `App` PascalCase. Update the two import specifiers `from "./App"` -> `from "./app"` in main.tsx:3 and app.test.tsx. No public/registry surface touched.
round: 1

### F-005 · high · dead-code · cli/diffgazer/src/hooks/use-key.ts:1-18, cli/diffgazer/src/app/providers/keyboard-provider.tsx:8-12, cli/diffgazer/src/app/providers/keyboard-provider.tsx:26-29, cli/diffgazer/src/app/providers/keyboard-provider.tsx:60-87, cli/diffgazer/src/app/providers/keyboard-provider.tsx:134-145
Dead hook `useKey` and its entire scoped-handler dispatch infrastructure in the keyboard provider
Evidence: `useKey` is exported but has ZERO importers anywhere in the repo. It is the SOLE consumer of `KeyboardContextValue.registerHandler`. Consequently the backing machinery in keyboard-provider.tsx is also dead: the `registerHandler` callback (60-87), the per-scope `ScopeEntry`/`scopesRef` handler registry (26-29, 40, 65-86), and the scoped-dispatch branch in the `useInput` handler (134-145). Nothing populates `scopesRef`, so that branch never fires. Live components route keys only through `registerGlobalHandler` and `useScope` push/pop.
Fix: Delete cli/diffgazer/src/hooks/use-key.ts. In keyboard-provider.tsx remove `registerHandler` from `KeyboardContextValue` (8-12) and the value object, delete the `ScopeEntry` interface (26-29), the `scopesRef` ref (40), the `registerHandler` useCallback (60-87), and the scoped-dispatch branch in `useInput` (134-145), keeping only the global-handler dispatch path. Keep `pushScope`/`popScope`/`activeScope`.
round: 1

### F-007 · high · barrels · libs/core/src/api/review.ts:1-8, libs/core/src/review/stream-review.ts, libs/core/src/onboarding/defaults.ts:1-2, libs/core/src/providers/list.ts:5-6, libs/core/src/schemas/config/capabilities.ts:2-8, libs/core/package.json:11-135
libs/core imports its own package through its subpath exports 95 times (forbidden self-barrel imports)
Evidence: `rg "from \"@diffgazer/core" libs/core/src` returns 95 import statements across 58 files. tsconfig.json has NO path alias, so `@diffgazer/core/*` resolves through the package `exports` map to compiled `dist/`. This is the exact pattern D6 forbids and sota-structure marks FORBIDDEN. It makes the package self-referential at build time: src must compile against its own dist.
Fix: Rewrite all 95 intra-package `@diffgazer/core/<subpath>` imports inside libs/core/src to relative paths (e.g. `@diffgazer/core/schemas/review` -> `../schemas/review/index.js`). Use a ts-morph codemod. Then wire the D6 lint ban on self-package barrel/subpath imports so it cannot regress.
round: 1

### F-011 · high · dry · libs/ui/tsup.config.ts:24-28, libs/ui/tsup.config.ts:34, libs/ui/scripts/build-declarations.ts:44-48, libs/ui/scripts/build-declarations.ts:40-42
registryItemToDistKey() and keys-hook detection duplicated byte-for-byte between tsup.config.ts and scripts/build-declarations.ts
Evidence: registryItemToDistKey is identical in both files (verified char-for-char). build-declarations.ts:36-42 carries the comment 'Mirror tsup's keys-hook detection' and re-derives the same Set via extractDiffgazerKeysHookNames + `use-` prefix that tsup.config.ts:34 derives as DIFFGAZER_KEYS_HOOKS. A real named concept duplicated across two build entry points, kept in sync only by a comment.
Fix: Promote registryItemToDistKey and the keys-hook Set derivation into @diffgazer/registry as a single exported helper, e.g. registryItemToDistKey(item) and resolveKeysHookFiles(items). Import both in tsup.config.ts and build-declarations.ts. Removes the 'mirror' comment and the drift risk.
round: 1

### F-012 · high · architecture · cli/server/src/shared/middlewares/setup-guard.ts:3, cli/server/src/features/config/service.ts:47, cli/server/src/features/review/router.ts:6, cli/server/src/shared/middlewares/trust-guard.ts:3
cli/server shared-tier middleware setup-guard.ts imports features/config/service.ts (shared -> feature wrong-direction import)
Evidence: setup-guard.ts:3 does `import { getSetupStatus } from "../../features/config/service.js"`. setup-guard.ts lives in shared/middlewares/ and is consumed by features/review/router.ts. So the import graph is review(feature) -> shared/middlewares -> config(feature): the shared tier depends on a feature, inverting the unidirectional rule. getSetupStatus only reads getStore() from shared/lib/config/store.js; the sibling trust-guard.ts already does the correct shared->shared import.
Fix: Move getSetupStatus (plus its isKeyReadable helper) into cli/server/src/shared/lib/config/ (e.g. shared/lib/config/setup-status.ts). Update setup-guard.ts to import it from `../lib/config/setup-status.js` (shared->shared), and have features/config/service.ts import it from shared as well. Net result: middleware and feature both depend downward on shared; no shared->feature edge remains.
round: 1

### F-013 · high · hygiene · package.json:22, biome.root.json:1-43, apps/docs/package.json:19, apps/web/package.json, libs/ui/package.json, cli/server/package.json
Biome lint covers only apps/docs + scripts/monorepo — 9 of 10 workspaces are never linted
Evidence: Root `check` script is `biome lint --config-path=biome.root.json scripts/monorepo && turbo run check`. biome.root.json is named so Biome will NOT auto-discover it; the only package defining a check/lint task is apps/docs. Grepped every workspace package.json: apps/web, apps/landing, cli/add, cli/server, cli/diffgazer, libs/core, libs/keys, libs/ui, libs/registry have NO check/lint/format script. So `pnpm run check` lints only scripts/monorepo + apps/docs/src. The entire source of the other 9 workspaces is never Biome-linted. This blocks the planned D-enforcement filename-case + barrel-ban rules.
Fix: Add a check/lint script invoking biome to every workspace package.json (or a single root `biome lint .` over the whole tree using one discoverable root config), and define a per-package check turbo task so `turbo run check` fans out to all workspaces. Rename biome.root.json to biome.json at root so it is auto-discovered, or keep --config-path consistently in every package's lint script.
round: 1

### F-134 · low · naming · cli/server/src/dev.ts:1-27, cli/server/package.json, cli/server/src/http-server.ts:1-20, cli/server/src/index.ts:1-4

Evidence: cli/server/src/dev.ts is the only file that wires createApp() + startDevServer() + SIGTERM/SIGINT shutdown into a runnable serve entry. package.json runs it as BOTH `"dev": "tsx src/dev.ts"` AND `"start": "node dist/dev.js"` — i.e. dev.ts is also the PRODUCTION serve entry. The Hono guidance requires the createApp() factory to be separate from a well-named serve entry; the name implies dev-only while it serves production. The embedded server imports createApp from the index.ts lib entry, never from dev.ts.
Fix: Rename cli/server/src/dev.ts to cli/server/src/serve.ts, and update the dev (tsx src/serve.ts) and start (node dist/serve.js) scripts in package.json plus the benchmark-server.mjs comment. Keep app.ts (factory) and index.ts (lib entry) unchanged.
round: 2

### F-135 · low · mirror · cli/diffgazer/src/app/back-navigation.ts:1-19, apps/web/src/lib/back-navigation.ts:1, cli/diffgazer/src/lib/list-navigation.ts:1, cli/diffgazer/src/lib/highlight-navigation.ts:1, cli/diffgazer/src/app/navigation-context.tsx:5
cli/diffgazer/src/app/back-navigation.ts is pure routing logic stranded in app/; the same-role file in apps/web lives in lib/
Evidence: Both back-navigation files play the identical role: pure, JSX-free route-resolution helpers wrapping @diffgazer/core/navigation's getBackTarget. apps/web places this in the app-shared lib/ tier; cli/diffgazer places it loose at app/ root. The app/ dir is reserved for providers + router + thin routes/screens. diffgazer's own lib/ ALREADY holds its peer navigation logic (list-navigation.ts, highlight-navigation.ts). The only consumer is app/navigation-context.tsx.
Fix: Move cli/diffgazer/src/app/back-navigation.ts -> cli/diffgazer/src/lib/back-navigation.ts (alongside list-navigation.ts and highlight-navigation.ts, matching apps/web). Update the single import in app/navigation-context.tsx via ts-morph in the pure-move phase.
round: 2

round: 2

### F-137 · medium · barrels · libs/ui/tsup.config.ts:38-56, libs/ui/scripts/build-declarations.ts:203-234, libs/ui/package.json:289-294, libs/ui/package.json:300-318
@diffgazer/ui builds and packs 18 dist entries that are not in the exports map — unreachable dead pack weight behind a fragile files deny-list
Evidence: tsup.config.ts:38-50 auto-discovers a dist entry for EVERY non-theme registry.json item, and build-declarations.ts writes a public .d.ts for every item. The build produces 85 dist entries, but the exports map exposes only 64 subpaths. 18 entries are BUILT and shipped (files:["dist"]) yet have no exports path (keys-mirror hooks use-navigation/use-focus-restore/etc, dead lib/focus & lib/resolve-tab-target, 10 internal libs like lib/aria-utils/lib/diff/lib/search). README documents only the 64. The only mitigation is a manual files deny-list that misses all 18, and no validator catches the gap.
Fix: Restrict emitted entries to the curated set that backs the exports map (drive both tsup and build-declarations off the same allowlist, or a meta.packageEntry flag in registry.json) so keys-mirror hooks, dead lib/focus & lib/resolve-tab-target, and internal variant/helper libs no longer become orphaned dist entries. Then delete the fragile files deny-list. Add a build-time assertion that the set of dist *.js entry points equals the set of exports-map import targets.
round: 2

### F-142 · high · tests · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/src/testing/factories.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/src/api/config.test.ts
Vitest-importing test helper testing/factories.ts ships in the published @diffgazer/core tarball but is unreachable and single-internal-consumer
Evidence: testing/factories.ts:1 does `import { vi } from "vitest"` at module top and exports only `createMockClient()`. tsconfig.json:6 excludes only `**/*.test.ts` and `**/__fixtures__/**` (NOT `**/testing/**`), so `src/testing/factories.ts` compiles into `dist/testing/factories.js` with a hard top-level vitest import. package.json has no `files` field, so the whole package (dist included) is published; yet `factories.ts` is NOT in the `exports` map (package.json:132-135 exposes only `./testing/dom-polyfills`), making it unreachable by any consumer. Its sole in-repo consumer is core's own `api/config.test.ts:` (`import { createMockClient } from "../testing/factories.js"`); the cross-package `makeIssue` factories are separate per-package files (apps/web/src/testing/factories.ts, cli/server/src/shared/lib/testing/factories.ts), confirming nothing outside core imports `@diffgazer/core/testing/factories`. This is the same class of leak as F-110 (keys dist/testing/* vitest leak) but a distinct file/package. Note dom-polyfills.ts (also vitest-importing) is legitimately exported and consumed by web/landing test-setup, so it is correct — the asymmetry is exactly the tell that factories.ts is dead tarball weight.
Fix: Colocate the helper with its only consumer: move createMockClient into libs/core/src/api/config.test.ts (or a sibling api/testing-helpers.ts that the build excludes), delete src/testing/factories.ts. Independently, add `**/testing/**` (or a `files` allowlist) to the published-build exclude so test-only modules can never reach dist, matching the keys remediation.
round: 3

Fix: Fold styles/ removal into the D5 mirror-removal task: delete the apps/docs/styles/ materialization and its generator path in scripts/monorepo/artifacts/sync.mjs (getMaterializedPrimaryStylesContent, materializePrimaryStylesFromArtifact, collectPrimaryStyleErrors). Change apps/docs/src/index.css to `@import "@diffgazer/ui/sources.css"; @import "@diffgazer/ui/styles.css";` (matching consumption-metadata.ts:139), drop the now-dead `styles/` line from apps/docs/.gitignore:13 and the `styles/styles.css` requiredRootFiles entry at sync.mjs:378. The D5 spec must list apps/docs/styles/ as a sibling removal alongside apps/docs/registry/.

### F-147 · low · naming · libs/registry/src/logger.ts, libs/registry/src/cli/logger.ts

### F-152 · medium · tests · cli/diffgazer/src/cli-options.test.ts, cli/diffgazer/src/cli-options.ts, cli/diffgazer/src/lib/servers/embedded-server.test.ts, cli/diffgazer/src/lib/servers/server-factories.test.ts, cli/diffgazer/src/web-launcher.test.ts

Evidence: Per context.md §3, `libs/ui/registry/lib/testing/` exists to QUARANTINE tests of registry-DISTRIBUTED `registry/lib/*` source out of the copy/shadcn handoff bundle. Of its 13 tests, 10 mirror a real `registry/lib/<x>.ts` source; 3 are build-tooling tests with NO `registry/lib` source pair (verified phantom): `registry-validators.test.ts` imports `../../../src/validation/registry-validation-fs`, `registry-exports-validator`, `registry-import-validator` (the F-010 build-time validators); `validate-registry-metadata.test.ts` spawns `libs/ui/scripts/validate-registry-metadata.ts` via execFileSync; `ui-three-path-readiness.test.ts` imports `../../../scripts/transform-public-registry-keys-imports` (the F-053 4-hyphen build script). The 6 build scripts in `libs/ui/scripts/` and the 4 validators in `libs/ui/src/validation/` have ZERO colocated tests (verified `libs/ui/scripts/*.test.*` and `libs/ui/src/**/*.test.*` are empty) — these 3 are their only test homes, located 3 levels away inside the registry distribution quarantine.
Fix: Move these 3 build-tooling tests out of the registry quarantine and colocate them with their source after F-010's validation-shell relocation: `registry-validators.test.ts` -> beside the validators (e.g. `libs/ui/src/validation/registry-exports-validator.test.ts` etc., or one `validators.test.ts` if F-010 consolidates them), and `validate-registry-metadata.test.ts` + `ui-three-path-readiness.test.ts` -> `libs/ui/scripts/<script>.test.ts` next to the scripts they exercise (named to match each source stem). The registry/lib/testing/ folder then holds only tests for actually-distributed registry/lib code.
round: 4

### F-156 · low · naming · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/src/hooks/use-servers.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/src/hooks/use-exit.ts

Evidence: cli/diffgazer/src/hooks/use-servers.ts (29 lines) exports two symbols: `useServers(...)` (the hook) and `stopAllServers(): Promise<void>` (a module-level async function operating on module state, NOT a hook). stopAllServers is imported by the sibling use-exit.ts:4,21 — a non-hook value pulled from a use- prefixed file. The use- prefix is a React-tooling signal (lint rules-of-hooks key off it); a file that also exports a non-hook imperative server-shutdown function under that prefix mislabels half its surface. Confusable-pair note: use-exit.ts (useExit, imperative exit) and use-exit-handler.ts (useExitHandler, wires signals/Ctrl-C) are a second confusable pair in the same tier, though they are legitimately layered.

This keeps the use- prefix reserved for the hook export only.
round: 4

### F-159 · low · naming · libs/core/src/api/hooks/use-review-lifecycle-base.ts, libs/core/src/api/hooks/index.ts, apps/web/src/features/review/hooks/use-review-lifecycle.ts, cli/diffgazer/src/features/review/hooks/use-review-lifecycle.ts

The `-base` suffix names an implementation relationship ('the shared thing the two real hooks wrap'), not a concept — exactly the kind of suffix the policy treats as a rename/split smell. It is consumed by `apps/web/src/features/review/hooks/use-review-lifecycle.ts` and `cli/diffgazer/src/features/review/hooks/use-review-lifecycle.ts`, both named `use-review-lifecycle` without a suffix, so the shared core hook collides conceptually with the per-app wrappers and resorts to `-base` to disambiguate. Fix: Rename to name the actual concept the core hook owns, e.g. `use-review-lifecycle-controller.ts` -> better, `use-review-lifecycle-machine.ts` if it owns the state machine, or fold it into `review/review-state.ts`/api-hooks naming. Update the `libs/core/src/api/hooks/index.ts` re-export and both app wrappers in the same lockstep commit.
round: 4

### F-160 · low · naming · cli/server/src/shared/lib/config/store.ts, cli/server/src/shared/lib/config/state.ts, cli/server/src/shared/lib/config/secrets-store.ts, cli/server/src/shared/lib/config/trust-store.ts, cli/server/src/shared/lib/config/providers-state.ts

Not in the digest. A reader cannot tell from the basename which file owns the singleton vs the persistence functions.

round: 4

### F-167 · medium · mirror · cli/diffgazer/src/features/review/components/severity-bar.tsx, cli/diffgazer/src/features/review/components/severity-breakdown.tsx, cli/diffgazer/src/features/review/components/progress-list.tsx, cli/diffgazer/src/features/review/components/progress-step.tsx, cli/diffgazer/src/features/history/components/history-insights-pane.tsx, apps/web/src/components/ui/severity/severity-bar.tsx, apps/web/src/components/ui/severity/severity-breakdown.tsx, apps/web/src/components/ui/progress/progress-list.tsx

### F-174 · low · architecture · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/turbo.json

Evidence: cli/diffgazer/package.json:37-38 builds and embeds the web SPA (`build:deps` runs `--filter=@diffgazer/web`; `build:web` runs `pnpm --filter @diffgazer/web exec ... vite build --outDir ../../cli/diffgazer/dist/web`), yet `@diffgazer/web` appears in neither `dependencies` nor `devDependencies` (package.json:49-76 — only core/keys/server are declared). The web build edge exists only because turbo.json:18-21 hardcodes `"diffgazer#build": { "dependsOn": ["^build", "@diffgazer/web#build"] }`. So the cross-workspace build ordering is encoded in two places (a manual turbo edge plus two filtered pnpm invocations) instead of one package-graph dependency edge. If the explicit turbo edge is ever dropped, `^build` alone will not order the web build, because the package graph has no `@diffgazer/web` edge to derive it from.
Fix: Add `"@diffgazer/web": "workspace:*"` to cli/diffgazer devDependencies (it is a build-time embed, bundled output not an importable package, so devDependencies is correct). Then the `^build` graph edge orders the web build naturally and the explicit `@diffgazer/web#build` entry in turbo.json:19 becomes redundant and can be removed, collapsing the ordering to a single source of truth.
round: 4

### F-181 · medium · hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/tsconfig/base.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/tsconfig.test.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/add/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/add/tsconfig.test.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/tsconfig.json
moduleResolution drift among Node-targeting workspaces: cli/server emits dist via tsc using Bundler resolution while cli/add and libs/registry use NodeNext, and source/test configs disagree within a package
Evidence: base.json sets moduleResolution:"Bundler". cli/server/tsconfig.json builds with `tsc` (package.json build:"tsc", outDir:dist, emits runnable Node ESM at dist/dev.js) yet inherits Bundler resolution via node.json->base.json — Bundler mode is for no-emit/bundled contexts, not for emitting Node ESM. Its own cli/server/tsconfig.test.json overrides back to module/moduleResolution NodeNext (lines 6-7), acknowledging the mismatch only for tests. Meanwhile sibling Node emitters set NodeNext directly: libs/registry/tsconfig.json (build:"tsc") uses module/moduleResolution NodeNext, and cli/add/tsconfig.json uses NodeNext — but cli/add/tsconfig.test.json extends cli-test.json (->base.json) which is Bundler, so cli/add's source=NodeNext but tests=Bundler. So three Node CLI/lib packages disagree on resolution strategy, and two of them disagree with their own test config.
Fix: Standardize the Node-emitting packages on NodeNext: change cli/server/tsconfig.json to module/moduleResolution NodeNext (matching its tsc emit and its own test config), and make cli/add/tsconfig.test.json inherit NodeNext (introduce a node-test preset rather than reusing the Bundler-based cli-test.json). Keep Bundler only for the no-emit/vite/tsup-bundled surfaces (apps, libs/ui, libs/keys, cli/diffgazer).

### F-182 · medium · hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/biome.root.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/biome.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/package.json

### F-189 · medium · hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/add/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/keys/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/tsconfig/node.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/tsconfig/base.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/tsconfig/react.json

Evidence: A shared tsconfig preset library exists at libs/core/tsconfig/ (base.json: target ES2022 / module ESNext / moduleResolution Bundler / lib ES2022; node.json + react.json extend it). It IS extended by cli/server/tsconfig.json:2, cli/diffgazer/tsconfig.json:2, libs/core/tsconfig.json:2, and the *.test.json / scripts/tsconfig.json configs (cli/add/tsconfig.test.json:3, cli/add/scripts/tsconfig.json:2, cli/server/tsconfig.test.json:3). But the MAIN tsconfig.json of cli/add, libs/keys, libs/ui, libs/registry have NO `extends` and hand-inline compilerOptions, producing two concrete drifts: (a) module/moduleResolution — cli/add/tsconfig.json:7-8 and libs/registry/tsconfig.json:4-5 inline module/moduleResolution `NodeNext`, directly contradicting base.json's Bundler default they would otherwise inherit (the behavioral half of this is confirmed F-181, but the structural root cause — bypassing the preset that exists for exactly this — is not flagged); (b) lib version — libs/ui/tsconfig.json:6 (and libs/ui/registry/tsconfig.json:7, libs/ui/tsconfig.tools.json:4, apps/docs/tsconfig.json:8) declare `lib: ["ES2023", ...]` while target stays ES2022 and every other workspace + all three presets use `lib: ["ES2022"]` (verified across all 14 tsconfigs). This ES2023-on-ES2022-target drift is NOT covered by any digest finding. The intra-package inconsistency is self-evidently wrong: cli/add/tsconfig.json inlines NodeNext while its own cli/add/tsconfig.test.json extends a Bundler-based preset.
Fix: Make the four main tsconfigs extend the shared presets instead of inlining: cli/add/tsconfig.json -> `extends: ../../libs/core/tsconfig/node.json` (drop the inline NodeNext unless a documented reason exists; if NodeNext is required for the dist emit, encode that as a `node-nodenext.json` preset and extend it); libs/registry/tsconfig.json -> same node preset; libs/keys/tsconfig.json and libs/ui/tsconfig.json -> `extends: ../../libs/core/tsconfig/react.json`, deleting the redundant inlined target/module/moduleResolution. Normalize `lib` to ES2022 in libs/ui/tsconfig.json:6, libs/ui/registry/tsconfig.json:7, libs/ui/tsconfig.tools.json:4, and apps/docs/tsconfig.json:8 (or bump the shared base.json/react.json lib to ES2023 once and let everyone inherit it) so target and lib agree repo-wide. Net effect: the preset library becomes the single source of truth and the F-181 moduleResolution drift plus the ES2023/ES2022 lib drift both resolve structurally.
round: 6

### F-193 · info · hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/biome.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/biome.root.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/src/catalog/catalog-snapshot.ts
No .editorconfig or .gitattributes — tab/space and line-ending drift is unenforced
Evidence: The repo has no .editorconfig and no .gitattributes (confirmed via rg --files). biome.root.json:11-13 disables the formatter (`formatter.enabled: false`) and apps/docs/biome.json is the only auto-discoverable config and sets tab indentation, so apps/docs source is tab-indented while every other workspace is space-indented (verified across the config files: apps/docs/vite.config.ts is tab-indented, all other vitest/tsup configs are space-indented) — the symptom F-182 flags as a biome-topology divergence. With the formatter off AND no editor-agnostic .editorconfig, nothing pins indentation for editors that do not read Biome, so the drift will recur on every new file. Separately, for a cross-platform CLI repo shipping bin/ scripts plus a committed 9242-line generated snapshot (libs/core/src/catalog/catalog-snapshot.ts) and committed public/r JSON, the absence of .gitattributes means no `* text=auto eol=lf` line-ending normalization and no `linguist-generated`/`-diff` marking for those generated trees, so they pollute diffs and language stats.
Fix: Add a root .editorconfig encoding the house style (root=true; `[*]` indent_style=space, indent_size=2, end_of_line=lf, insert_final_newline=true; `[apps/docs/**]` indent_style=tab if that divergence is intentional, otherwise converge docs to spaces and delete the standalone apps/docs/biome.json override — pairs with the F-182 fix). Add a root .gitattributes with `* text=auto eol=lf`, mark the generated trees `linguist-generated=true` and optionally `-diff` (libs/core/src/catalog/catalog-snapshot.ts, libs/ui/public/r/**, libs/keys/public/r/**, and the gitignored mirrors), so generated content stops inflating diffs and language stats.
round: 6

### F-194 · medium · hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/tsconfig.json
Plain-tsc production builds in cli/server and libs/registry compile colocated tests into dist/ (missing test exclude)
Evidence: Both packages have build script `"build": "tsc"` driving the default tsconfig.json with `include: ["src"]`. cli/server/tsconfig.json has NO `exclude` at all; libs/registry/tsconfig.json has `exclude: ["src/__tests__"]` — a dir that does not exist. Their colocated tests live in cli/server/src/*.test.ts and libs/registry/src/testing/*.test.ts, so neither exclude pattern catches them. Result: `cli/server/dist/` ships 8 compiled test artifacts (app.test.js, http-server.test.js, + maps/dts) and `libs/registry/dist/testing/` ships 19 compiled .test.js files (plus .d.ts/.d.ts.map). Both packages list vitest in devDependencies, so these test modules pull test-only imports into the consumed build. By contrast libs/core/tsconfig.json correctly does `exclude: ["node_modules","dist","**/*.test.ts","**/__fixtures__/**"]` and its dist has zero test files. Both leaking packages are private:true and consumed via workspace:* (registry by libs/ui, libs/keys, cli/add, apps/docs; server bundled into the diffgazer binary by tsup noExternal), so this is dead build weight + a quarantine failure rather than an npm-tarball leak. validate-artifacts.mjs:135 only guards the published @diffgazer/ui npm pack against forbidden files — it never inspects registry or server dist, so this leak is entirely unguarded. This is the same leak class as confirmed F-110 (keys) and F-142 (core test helper) but via a distinct root cause (missing/dead tsc exclude in two plain-tsc production builds).
Fix: Add `"exclude": ["**/*.test.ts", "node_modules", "dist"]` to cli/server/tsconfig.json. In libs/registry/tsconfig.json replace the dead `"exclude": ["src/__tests__"]` with `"exclude": ["**/*.test.ts", "src/testing", "node_modules", "dist"]` (matching the actual test home src/testing/). ### F-202 · low · hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/package.json

The root pnpm.overrides pins @types/node to ^25.2.3 (package.json:86). This is a sibling of confirmed F-181/F-189/F-195 toolchain-version drift, but against an explicitly documented rule rather than mere inconsistency.
Fix: Bump the @types/node devDependency range to ^25.2.3 in cli/diffgazer/package.json, cli/server/package.json, and libs/core/package.json to match the governance rule and the root override, then update the lockfile via pnpm. This is the exact case PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md:198 warns about.

Keep the exported symbol `ConsumptionBlock` unchanged (it is the public MDX tag referenced in MDX content and asserted by docs-library.test.ts), so no MDX/feature-mdx-components changes are needed. Fold this into F-029's batch so all 4 -block files lose the folder-echoing suffix in one pass. ### F-211 · low · naming · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/src/docs/index.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/src/docs/sync-operations.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/src/docs/loader.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/src/docs/cache.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/src/docs-data/build-docs-data.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/src/docs-data/build-components.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/src/docs-data/build-hooks.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/src/index.ts
libs/registry confusable sibling folders docs/ and docs-data/ split two unrelated concerns by a -data suffix
Evidence: libs/registry/src/ has two top-level sibling folders whose names differ only by a `-data` suffix yet hold unrelated concerns. `docs/` is the docs-SYNC engine: `docs/index.ts:13` exports `syncDocsFromArtifacts`, composing `docs/loader.ts` (loadLibraryArtifacts), `docs/sync-operations.ts` (354 lines, runDocsSyncPass — copies artifact JSON into a docs tree), `docs/cache.ts` (sync fingerprint/state), `docs/paths.ts`. `docs-data/` is the docs-DATA-GENERATION builders: `docs-data/index.ts` re-exports `buildDocsData`, `generateHooksSource`, `createDocsHighlighter`, `generateEnrichedHookData` from build-components.ts/build-hooks.ts/highlight.ts. The public entry index.ts exports both side by side (index.ts:28 `from "./docs/index.js"` for sync; index.ts:90/106/120 `from "./docs-data/index.js"` for the builders), so a reader at the package surface sees two near-identical folder names and must open both to learn which is the sync pass and which is the data builder. The digest already flags path-echo WITHIN docs-data (F-039 build-docs-data.ts, F-040 docs-data/utils.ts) and the docs/index.ts orchestrator name (F-018), but no existing finding addresses the confusable docs/ vs docs-data/ folder-name collision itself.
Fix: Rename the two folders to name their distinct concepts rather than overloading the `docs` stem. Rename `docs/` -> `docs-sync/` (it owns syncDocsFromArtifacts + loader/sync-operations/cache/paths) and keep `docs-data/` as the builders, OR rename `docs-data/` -> `docs-build/` and keep `docs/`. Public export symbols stay unchanged; only the internal folder path moves.

### F-213 · medium · hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/keys/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/keys/internal-docs-manifest.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/internal-docs-manifest.json

The file stays in the repo for build tooling; it just should not be published. ### F-215 · high · boundaries · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/src/components/layout/header.tsx, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/src/get-figlet.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/registry/ui/logo/get-figlet-text.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md
Browser SPA (apps/web) imports the Node-only eager figlet renderer @diffgazer/core/get-figlet, bundling figlet+Big.js into the web bundle against PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md:176 and the module's own doc-comment, with figlet undeclared as an apps/web dependency
Evidence: Trace: apps/web/src/components/layout/header.tsx:2 imports `getFigletText` from `@diffgazer/core/get-figlet` and calls it at module-init (line 45: `const WORDMARK_ASCII = getFigletText(WORDMARK_TEXT)`) to compute the browser wordmark, then passes the result to the ui `Logo` component's `asciiText` prop (lines 47-50). libs/core/src/get-figlet.ts:1-3 imports `figlet` and `figlet/importable-fonts/Big.js` as HARD, EAGER deps; its own doc-comment (lines 5-15) states it is the 'synchronous figlet banner renderer for the Node CLI' and that it 'intentionally diverges from the browser counterpart in libs/ui/registry/ui/logo/get-figlet-text.ts, which loads figlet ... via async dynamic import() because figlet is an optional peer there and must be code-split out of the browser bundle' — explicitly warning the two strategies must not be forced onto each other's runtime. libs/core/package.json:80 exports `./get-figlet` and declares `figlet: ^1.10.0` as a hard dependency. apps/web/package.json declares NO `figlet` dependency (verified: phantom dependency resolved only transitively through @diffgazer/core). PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md:176 mandates: 'The default @diffgazer/ui/components/logo entry must not import figlet; it accepts precomputed asciiText instead' — the governance pattern is a precomputed-ascii browser path with figlet code-split out, which apps/web defeats by precomputing via the Node eager renderer. The ui browser-async variant (libs/ui/registry/ui/logo/get-figlet-text.ts, exported as @diffgazer/ui/components/logo/figlet) already exists for exactly this case. This is distinct from R-023 (which flagged only the placement of get-figlet.ts at libs/core root, not a browser consumer) and F-049/F-212 (basename/SVG).
Fix: Stop importing @diffgazer/core/get-figlet from the browser. Either (a) have apps/web/src/components/layout/header.tsx derive its wordmark via the ui async optional-peer path `@diffgazer/ui/components/logo/figlet` (and declare `figlet` as an apps/web dependency, matching apps/docs which already declares figlet ^1.10.0), or (b) pass a precomputed static ascii constant to `Logo` per PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md:176. Scope `@diffgazer/core/get-figlet` to Node/CLI consumers only — cli/diffgazer/src/banner.ts is the legitimate consumer. This keeps figlet+Big.js out of the browser bundle and removes the undeclared transitive dependency in apps/web.
round: 9

### F-216 · low · build-flow / hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/keys/scripts/verify-rsc-directives.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/tsup.config.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/keys/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/package.json
Divergent, unshared RSC "use client" build-verification patterns across the two React-publishing libs
Evidence: The two sibling dual-publish React libraries enforce the same concern (correct `"use client"` directives in dist output) with two divergent, non-shared mechanisms. libs/keys ships a dedicated post-build step `verify:rsc` -> scripts/verify-rsc-directives.ts (wired into its `build` script: `... pnpm verify:rsc ...` in libs/keys/package.json), and that script hand-maintains an 11-path allowlist (`const clientOutputs = ["dist/index.js", "dist/providers/keyboard-provider.js", "dist/hooks/use-key.js", ...]` at verify-rsc-directives.ts:6-18) that must be manually kept in lockstep with every new client hook/provider added to src/. libs/ui instead derives client entries from registry metadata at build time inside tsup.config.ts (inject loop at lines 155-170 driven by `item.meta?.client`, plus an explicit client/server-decision validation at line 172+), and carries NO `verify:rsc` script or post-build directive guard in its `build` pipeline (libs/ui/package.json build = `... tsup && pnpm build:declarations && pnpm build:shadcn ...`). So the smaller-surface lib uses a brittle hardcoded list while the 321-`use client`-source lib uses a registry-driven approach; neither shares the logic, and the keys allowlist is the kind of manually-synced artifact that silently drifts when a hook is added or removed. Not a correctness bug today (the keys allowlist currently matches its real exports), but a build-flow consistency gap the digest's build-script DRY findings (F-011 tsup/build-declarations dup, F-175 verify-dist-esm dup, F-137 ui pack entries) did not cover.
Fix: Pick one RSC-directive verification mechanism for both dual-publish React libs and own it in @diffgazer/registry. Preferred: replace the hardcoded `clientOutputs` allowlist in libs/keys/scripts/verify-rsc-directives.ts with a registry-metadata-driven check (mirroring libs/ui's `item.meta?.client` source of truth), and expose the shared check (e.g. `assertRscClientDirectives({ rootDir, registryPath })`) from @diffgazer/registry so both libs call it from their `build` script. At minimum, add the same post-build `verify:rsc` guard to libs/ui so the larger client surface is also verified, and derive the keys list from registry metadata so adding a client hook cannot silently bypass the check.
round: 9

### F-217 · medium · config · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/vite.config.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/src/features/home/components/home-view.test.tsx, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/src/components/source-viewer.test.tsx, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/vitest.config.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/src/test-setup.ts
apps/docs vitest config lacks the global jsdom environment + setupFiles every other React-test surface has, forcing per-file pragma ceremony

Every sibling React surface instead sets this ONCE globally: apps/web/vitest.config.ts and apps/landing/vitest.config.ts use `environment: "jsdom"` + `setupFiles: ["./src/test-setup.ts"]`; libs/ui/vitest.config.ts uses the jsdom project + `setupFiles: ["./test-setup.ts"]`. The drift is brittle: a new docs component test that forgets the `// @vitest-environment jsdom` pragma silently runs under node and fails at the first `document` access. This is distinct from F-165 (which only covers test-setup.ts file PLACEMENT among web/landing/ui and never mentions docs having none) and from the F-003/F-143/D5 registry-mirror work (this is docs' own src test config, unrelated to the registry/ mirror).

In apps/docs/vite.config.ts, change the `test: isVitest ? {...}` object to include `environment: "jsdom"` and `setupFiles: ["./src/test-setup.ts"]` alongside the existing typecheck section. Create apps/docs/src/test-setup.ts mirroring apps/web/src/test-setup.ts (`import "@testing-library/jest-dom/vitest"`; `afterEach(cleanup)`). Then delete the now-redundant `// @vitest-environment jsdom` pragma lines and inline `import "@testing-library/jest-dom/vitest"` / per-file afterEach(cleanup) from the 6 affected docs test files. The 3 pure-node script tests (scripts/**/*.test.ts) keep working under jsdom or can be split into a node project if needed.
round: 9

### F-226 · high · boundaries / hygiene (cross-package dev-tooling contract) · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/vitest.config.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/test-setup.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/landing/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/package.json
Test runner (vitest) and DOM/RTL test tooling are undeclared phantom dependencies in 5 workspaces and version-drift across the rest
Evidence: Five workspaces run `vitest run` and import `vitest/config` yet declare NO `vitest`: apps/web, apps/landing, libs/ui, libs/core, cli/server (verified each package.json + vitest.config.ts). libs/ui is the worst: test-setup.ts:1-4 imports `@testing-library/jest-dom`, `@chialab/vitest-axe`, `@testing-library/react`, `vitest`, and vitest.config.ts uses `environment:'jsdom'` — yet libs/ui/package.json devDeps contain NONE of those runtimes (it even declares `@types/jsdom: ^28.0.3`, the types, while omitting `jsdom` itself — the smoking gun). They resolve only via the root-hoisted devDeps in package.json (`vitest ^4.1.0`, `@testing-library/react ^16.3.2`, `jsdom ^28.1.0`, `@chialab/vitest-axe ^0.19.1`). Where the tooling IS declared, it drifts: vitest `^4.0.0` (apps/docs) vs `^4.1.0` (keys/registry/add/diffgazer); jsdom `^27.0.0` (apps/docs) vs `^28.0.0` (web/landing/keys); @testing-library/react `^16.0.0`/`^16.2.0`/`^16.3.2`; @vitejs/plugin-react `^5.0.4` (docs) vs `^5.1.3` (web/landing). No `.npmrc` pins hoisting, so this is a default-hoist phantom-dependency contract that breaks under isolated linking or if root drops a tool. Distinct from F-144 (which is about the unused `test:types` typecheck wiring).
Fix: Declare every directly-imported test tool in each workspace's own devDependencies: add `vitest` to apps/web, apps/landing, libs/ui, libs/core, cli/server; add `jsdom` + `@testing-library/react` + `@testing-library/jest-dom` + `@chialab/vitest-axe` to libs/ui; add `@testing-library/react` (+ jsdom) to libs/core. Then pin one shared version repo-wide via a pnpm-workspace.yaml `catalog:` (or `pnpm.overrides`) for vitest/@testing-library*/jsdom/@vitejs/plugin-react and reference `catalog:` in each package, eliminating the ^4.0.0/^27/^16.0.0/^5.0.4 drift.
round: 10

### F-231 · medium · boundaries / shared configs (peer-type contract) · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/keys/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/package.json

### F-232 · medium · boundaries (library peer-dependency contract) · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/src/api/hooks/server.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/src/api/hooks/review.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/src/api/query-client.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/package.json
libs/core ships @tanstack/react-query as a hard dependency for its exported RQ hooks instead of a peerDependency (QueryClient-context singleton hazard)
Evidence: libs/core/package.json declares `react` as an (optional) peerDependency but `@tanstack/react-query ^5.80.7` as a hard `dependency`. Yet core exports React-Query-bound hooks (`src/api/hooks/{server,review,config}.ts`, `src/api/query-client.ts`) that call `useQuery`/`QueryClientProvider`, whose context is a singleton. Consumers apps/web and cli/diffgazer ALSO declare their own `@tanstack/react-query ^5.80.7` as a dependency. For a library exporting RQ hooks, react-query must be a peer (like react already is); as a hard dep it risks resolving a different react-query context instance than the consumer's `QueryClientProvider`, causing 'No QueryClient set' at runtime. It works today only because pnpm hoists one shared copy — fragile and contract-incorrect for the stated pre-publish hardening. The inconsistency (react = peer, the always-co-required react-query = hard dep) is the structural defect.
Fix: Move `@tanstack/react-query` from `dependencies` to `peerDependencies` in libs/core/package.json (mark optional via peerDependenciesMeta only if the RQ subpath is truly optional, matching the existing react treatment), keep it in devDependencies for type/test resolution, and rely on the consumers (apps/web, cli/diffgazer) that already declare it. This guarantees a single QueryClient context instance.
round: 10

### F-234 · high · dependency hygiene / library peer contract · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/registry/ui/accordion/accordion.tsx, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/registry/ui/popover/use-auto-focus.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/tsup.config.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/README.md
@diffgazer/ui marks @diffgazer/keys as an OPTIONAL peer, but two shipped package exports statically import it (governance + README self-contradiction)
Evidence: libs/ui/package.json:338-341 declares peerDependenciesMeta['@diffgazer/keys'].optional=true. But two SHIPPED, exported package entries statically import @diffgazer/keys at module top level: accordion.tsx:10 `import { getNavigationItems } from "@diffgazer/keys"` (export ./components/accordion, package.json:20) and popover/use-auto-focus.ts:4 `import { getFirstFocusableElement } from "@diffgazer/keys"` (bundled into export ./components/popover, package.json:204). tsup.config.ts:115-116 externalizes @diffgazer/keys and @diffgazer/keys/* in the npm build, so the static import survives into dist. Result: `npm install @diffgazer/ui` WITHOUT keys, then importing Accordion or Popover throws ERR_MODULE_NOT_FOUND at module resolution. Unlike figlet/lowlight (correctly optional because README:87,95 load them LAZILY via dynamic import() and fail only at call time), keys is imported eagerly and cannot be optional. This contradicts BOTH governing docs: PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md:175 states '@diffgazer/ui has REQUIRED React, React DOM, and @diffgazer/keys peers', and libs/ui/README.md:78 states '@diffgazer/keys is a REQUIRED peer for runtime package mode' — yet README.md:140 and the manifest both say optional. The README is internally inconsistent (line 78 required vs line 140 optional).
Fix: Make @diffgazer/keys a required peer of @diffgazer/ui: remove the '@diffgazer/keys' entry from peerDependenciesMeta in libs/ui/package.json (lines 338-341, keeping only figlet+lowlight optional). Then align libs/ui/README.md:140 and the 'Optional peers by entry' table to drop keys from the optional list, matching the already-correct README:78 and PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md:175. (Alternative, if optional truly desired: convert accordion.tsx and popover/use-auto-focus.ts keys imports to lazy dynamic import() with a call-time error, matching the figlet/lowlight pattern — but required peer is the simpler, governance-aligned fix for synchronously roving-focus components.)
round: 11

Consider a `sherif`/`syncpack`-style pinned-version policy (or pnpm overrides) so the React-app toolchain floor cannot drift per-workspace.
round: 11

### F-240 · info · dependency hygiene / version drift · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/package.json

### F-242 · medium · DRY · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/src/components/breadcrumbs.tsx, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/src/components/breadcrumbs.test.ts
breadcrumbs SECTIONS_WITH_INDEX is a hand-maintained 18-entry Set duplicating the content/docs filesystem, kept honest only by a repo-walking test
Evidence: breadcrumbs.tsx:11-30 declares `SECTIONS_WITH_INDEX = new Set([...18 hardcoded section paths...])` whose JSDoc says 'update both when adding/removing index.mdx files'. breadcrumbs.test.ts:15-31 then re-derives the SAME data from disk via `sectionsWithIndexOnDisk()` (readdirSync walk of content/docs for index.mdx) and asserts equality (line 40-42). The test's derivation IS the non-duplicated implementation: the Set should be computed (build-time/generated like the page tree) rather than hardcoded + guarded. This is a two-source-of-truth sync smell distinct from F-078 (color palette) and from F-184/F-073 (root-tooling tests); breadcrumbs is not mentioned for this in the digest.
Fix: Derive the section-with-index set from the same source.config/page-tree data that already drives docs-tree.ts (which knows which sections have index pages), or emit it during prepare:generated, eliminating the hardcoded Set. ### F-243 · medium · structure (colocation / rule-of-two) · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/src/hooks/use-config-guard.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/src/hooks/use-exit-handler.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/src/app/index.tsx, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/src/app/providers/server-provider.tsx

Both consumers live in `app/`, so neither hook is actually shared. This is the same stranded-shared-hook smell the digest already records for use-settings-zone (F-227, settings-only in shared hooks) and use-trust-form-keyboard (R-048, web), but these two cli/diffgazer hooks are uncovered (digest grep for use-config-guard/use-exit-handler returns only F-156, which is about use-servers.ts).
Fix: Colocate each with its sole consumer: move `use-config-guard.ts` into `src/app/` (next to index.tsx) and `use-exit-handler.ts` into `src/app/providers/` (next to server-provider.tsx); keep genuinely-shared hooks like use-terminal-dimensions/use-back-handler/use-scope in `src/hooks/`.
round: 11

### F-245 · medium · barrels · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/src/shared/lib/http/sse.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/src/shared/lib/http/types.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/src/features/review/sse-replay.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/src/features/review/service.test.ts

The SSEWriter interface itself lives in http/types.ts:1. This is the internal convenience-barrel / inconsistent-import smell D6 and the barrel table forbid — a within-package re-export that exists only to alias a type path. Distinct from any digest item (sse.ts/SSEWriter appear nowhere in digest.txt; F-117 grouped the stream sub-area files but never this re-export).

Repoint sse-replay.ts:3 and sse-replay.test.ts:4 to import `SSEWriter` from `../../shared/lib/http/types.js`, matching service.test.ts:10 so all consumers import the type from its single source module.

### F-251 · medium · dependency-hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/add/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/turbo.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/diffgazer/package.json
cli/add test script imperatively chains a cross-package build + bundle codegen instead of turbo dependsOn
Evidence: cli/add/package.json:56 defines "test": "pnpm --filter @diffgazer/registry build && pnpm run generate:bundles && vitest run". Every other package uses the clean "vitest run" (cli/server/package.json:17, libs/registry/package.json:32, cli/diffgazer/package.json:43). The cross-package build (@diffgazer/registry) and the local generate:bundles codegen (bundle-registry.ts + generate-keys-copy-bundle.ts, package.json:48) are prerequisites baked imperatively into the npm test script. turbo.json:25-28 already declares the test task with dependsOn:["^test"] but NOT "^build", so cli/add works around the missing wiring inline rather than declaring it. This couples test invocation to a hand-ordered shell chain and is invisible to turbo's dependency graph/caching.
Fix: Remove the imperative prefix so cli/add's test is just "vitest run". Wire the prerequisites declaratively: add "^build" (or a scoped registry build dep) to the test task's dependsOn in turbo.json, and make generate:bundles a turbo task that test dependsOn locally (the prebuild hook already runs generate:bundles before build), so the build graph — not the script string — orders the work.
round: 11

### F-252 · low · repo-hygiene · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/add/package.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/add/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/add/tsup.config.ts
cli/add dev script emits an un-bundled tsc dist that collides with the tsup-bundled dist the dgadd bin points to
Evidence: package.json:54 sets "dev": "tsc --watch", but tsconfig.json:22-24 sets outDir:"dist", rootDir:"src", noEmit:false — so dev emits a plain multi-file tsc build into dist/, while the real build (package.json:50) is "rm -rf dist && tsup ..." producing a single bundled dist/index.js, which is exactly what bin.dgadd (package.json:37) and files:["dist"] ship. Running dev therefore writes a structurally different, un-bundled artifact into the published output dir. Sibling CLIs avoid this: cli/diffgazer dev runs tsx (no emit), cli/server dev runs tsx src/dev.ts.
Fix: Make dev type-check-only ("tsc --noEmit --watch") or run via tsx like the other CLIs, so the watch loop never emits into the tsup-owned dist/. Keep dist/ exclusively a tsup build output.
round: 11

### F-255 · medium · build flow / turbo task-graph completeness · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/turbo.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/landing/src/content.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/deploy/landing.Dockerfile, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/docker-compose.yml
turbo.json @diffgazer/landing#build omits the VITE_DOCS_ORIGIN it bakes into the static bundle, breaking content-hash correctness (docs build proves the pattern)
Evidence: apps/landing Vite-inlines VITE_DOCS_ORIGIN into the static client build at build time (content.ts:11-12: `import.meta.env.VITE_DOCS_ORIGIN ?? "https://docs.b4r7.dev"`), and the deploy path passes it as an environment-specific Docker build arg (docker-compose.yml:66 `VITE_DOCS_ORIGIN: ${VITE_DOCS_ORIGIN:-https://docs.b4r7.dev}`; deploy/landing.Dockerfile ARG/ENV). But turbo.json's @diffgazer/landing#build task (lines 14-17) declares NO `env` array, while the sibling @diffgazer/docs#build task (line 11) correctly lists `env: ["REGISTRY_ORIGIN", "VITE_REGISTRY_ORIGIN", "VITE_PUBLIC_ORIGIN", "DOCS_PRERENDER", "DIFFGAZER_DEV"]`. turbo.json has no `globalEnv`; `globalPassThroughEnv` (line 3) only covers DIFFGAZER_SKIP_ARTIFACT_PREPARE. Therefore a landing build with a changed VITE_DOCS_ORIGIN does not invalidate turbo's content hash, so a cached dist/** with a stale docs origin is served. The docs task is the proof-of-pattern that the maintainers know VITE_* origins must be declared; landing (and, with the same gap, the generic `build` task that runs apps/web, which inlines VITE_API_URL + VITE_DIFFGAZER_SHUTDOWN_TOKEN per api.ts:18,21) is the inconsistency. Not in the digest — F-144/F-174/F-190 cover other turbo facets (test:types wiring, the cli/diffgazer→web edge, dead prepare:generated/check), none the build-env declaration.
Fix: Add `"env": ["VITE_DOCS_ORIGIN"]` to the @diffgazer/landing#build task in turbo.json (mirroring @diffgazer/docs#build), so the build-time origin participates in the cache key. For apps/web, add a `@diffgazer/web#build` override with `"env": ["VITE_API_URL", "VITE_DIFFGAZER_SHUTDOWN_TOKEN"]` (or, if these are never environment-baked for the embedded binary and are runtime-injected, document that explicitly so the omission is intentional rather than accidental).
round: 11

### F-256 · medium · boundaries · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/src/components/docs-mdx/feature-mdx-components.tsx, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/src/features/theme/components/color-grid.tsx, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/src/components/docs-mdx/index.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/docs/src/mdx-components.tsx
apps/docs shared components/ tier imports four feature components (shared→feature wrong-direction boundary violation)
Evidence: feature-mdx-components.tsx:3-6 lives in the app-shared `components/docs-mdx/` tier but statically imports four feature components straight out of `features/theme/components/`: ColorGrid, DiffgazerPreview, ThemePlayground, VariableDiagram. The sota-structure unidirectional rule is shared → features → app: the shared `components/` tier must be imported BY features, never import FROM a feature. The module is re-exported via docs-mdx/index.ts:8 and merged into the app-shell MDX map at mdx-components.tsx:3,9 (`...featureMdxComponents`), so this is route/app-shell wiring masquerading as a shared component — the `feature-` filename prefix (already noted as anomalous in R-068) is the tell. Verified by sweeping every apps/docs import of `@/features/` from non-feature code: routes/__root.tsx and routes/index.tsx import features (correct app→feature direction); layouts/header.tsx→features/search/search-context is already cited under F-241; only this file is a shared-tier→feature import, and it is NOT the home→search feature→feature case F-241 covers. F-014 flagged the barrel re-export and R-068 flagged the filename, but neither flags the import direction.
Fix: Move the MDX-component aggregation that binds theme feature components into the app/route tier (e.g. compose it where mdx-components.tsx assembles the final map, or have each theme feature contribute its own MDX wiring), so `components/docs-mdx/` stops importing downstream from `features/theme`. Concretely: relocate the ThemePlayground/VariableDiagram/ColorGrid/DiffgazerPreview entries (feature-mdx-components.tsx:3-6, 25-28) out of the shared docs-mdx module — keep only generic block components (Example, PropsTable, etc.) in the shared tier and merge the feature components at the app-shell composition point in mdx-components.tsx. Wire a dependency-cruiser rule forbidding `apps/docs/src/components` → `apps/docs/src/features` to prevent regression (aligns with the D-enforcement plan).
round: 12

### F-257 · low · structure · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/src/features/health/router.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/src/app.ts
cli/server features/health/ is a single-file feature folder for one trivial route
Evidence: cli/server/src/features/health/ contains exactly one 12-line source file (router.ts), which defines a single `/health` GET route returning {status:'ok',timestamp}. Verified by enumerating every feature folder's source-file count: config=3, git=3, health=1, review=22, settings=2, shutdown=2 — health is the only single-file feature folder. The feature is mounted in createApp at app.ts:124-125 (`app.route('/', healthRouter)` and `app.route('/api', healthRouter)`). D2 states 'a unit earns a folder at 3+ files' and sota-structure says 'a folder never gets created just because it exists'. The other features earn their folders via the {router,service,schemas[,test]} triad; health has only a router with no service/schema/test, so the folder wrapping adds a directory hop for one route. The digest never mentions 'health' (confirmed by grepping the full digest); F-036 covered only review-routes.ts naming, not this folder. This is a genuine, un-flagged structural inconsistency.
Fix: Flatten cli/server/src/features/health/router.ts to a single flat module cli/server/src/features/health.ts (dropping the single-child folder), and update the two import sites in app.ts (line 10 import and lines 124-125 mounts) to reference './features/health.js'. Keep the exported `healthRouter` name. This matches the doctrine's flat-sibling-until-3-files rule while preserving the per-route-group app.route() Hono convention.
round: 12

Fold this into the D8/doc-sync phase alongside F-101/F-141/F-223/F-228 so all doc-vs-tree drift is corrected together.
round: 14

## Rejected — do not re-report, do not re-judge

### R-001 · architecture · libs/core/src/schemas/config/capabilities.ts:2-8, libs/core/src/catalog/capabilities.ts:1, libs/core/src/catalog/transform.ts:1, libs/core/src/catalog/provider-overlay.ts:1
schemas/config <-> catalog cyclic dependency masked by self-subpath imports
Rejection reason: Import edges at the cited lines are factually real, BUT the back-edge (catalog -> schemas/config) is `import type` in ALL production code. `import type` is fully erased by TS and emits nothing to dist/*.js, so the compiled module graph is strictly unidirectional (config -> catalog). There is NO runtime circular dependency. The claim of 'a genuine 2-module domain cycle' at HIGH severity is overstated — a type-only cross-reference is the canonical benign case dependency-cruiser's no-circular rule supports ignoring. The actionable core is a logic-bearing domain-ownership refactor chasing a non-existent runtime cycle, i.e. churn. The genuine concern it leans on (self-package subpath imports) is already enumerated by F-007 and codified by D6. Uncertain-leaning-to-overstated + duplicate-of-D6-mechanism + churny domain-ownership fix => reject.
round: 1

### R-002 · naming · libs/ui/registry/examples/dialog/dialog-custom-trigger.tsx, libs/ui/registry/examples/diff-view/diff-view-default.tsx, libs/ui/registry/examples/stepper/stepper-variant-bullet.tsx, libs/ui/registry/examples/icons/chevron-default.tsx, libs/ui/scripts/build-docs-data.ts:89-94, libs/ui/registry/component-docs/dialog.ts:76, libs/ui/docs/content/components/stepper.mdx:45

Rejection reason: The 237/242 path-echo count is factually exact and the basename-as-key claim is real. But the diagnosis (pure path-echo, prefix is redundant) is wrong about causation, and the proposed fix would BREAK the build. generateDemoIndex builds a single FLAT global Record keyed by the bare example basename across ALL components with explicit collision detection. The folder prefix is the disambiguator that keeps each basename unique in that global namespace. The fix (drop the folder-name prefix) without rekeying generateDemoIndex to folder-qualified keys would collapse 41 components' default.tsx into ONE colliding key. As written the fix is churn that breaks the demo index and the MDX <Example name> contract, so reject.
round: 1

JS Array.prototype.sort is stable, so a rank-only re-sort preserves the server's tiebreak; the TUI test confirms stable ordering. There is no observable non-determinism. The proposed fix would actively CHANGE UI behavior, motivated by a refuted premise, and reaches across the cli/server feature-backend layer. Only web+TUI are genuine duplicates of each other, overlapping F-084's cluster. Refuted central evidence => reject.

### R-010 · dry · apps/docs/src/lib/docs-library.ts:51-80, apps/docs/src/lib/consumption-metadata.ts:56-141

The only shared literal is the short stable prefix. Forcing getConsumptionMetadata to reuse getLocalInstallCommand would couple two divergent normalization paths. AGENTS.md: 'Do not extract a helper only because two files look similar'; candidate itself rates this borderline-low. Churn, not improvement.
round: 1

### R-020 · architecture · libs/keys/artifacts/scripts/copy-artifacts.mjs:1-13, libs/keys/artifacts/package.json:13-19, libs/keys/scripts/build-publish-artifacts.ts:107-112, scripts/monorepo/validate-artifacts.mjs:228-232, PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE.md:155, apps/docs/config/docs-libraries.json:24-26
Nested @diffgazer/keys-artifacts workspace's build script duplicates the parent package's own copy step
Rejection reason: The central factual claim — 'NO pipeline ever invokes the nested workspace's build' — is FALSE. Root package.json:16 defines `"build":"turbo run build"` and release-readiness.yml runs it. Turbo's build task is global across every workspace member with a build script. The nested @diffgazer/keys-artifacts package.json HAS a build script (node scripts/copy-artifacts.mjs), so `turbo run build` DOES invoke it, with dependsOn:[^build]. The two copy calls are not redundant duplicates: the parent serves prepare:library-artifacts, while copy-artifacts.mjs lets the nested package populate its OWN dist as a first-class turbo graph node — correct turborepo hygiene. The parity check is a real regression guard, not tautological. The proposed fix would BREAK turbo graph participation and weaken validation. Existence is sanctioned by context.md/PACKAGE_GOVERNANCE/check-invariants. Premise wrong; not in scope.
round: 2

### R-021 · naming · libs/ui/docs/content/integrations/keys-focus.mdx, libs/ui/docs/content/integrations/keys-navigation.mdx, libs/ui/docs/content/integrations/keys-usekey.mdx, libs/ui/docs/content/integrations/keys-utilities.mdx, libs/ui/docs/content/integrations/keys-patterns.mdx, libs/ui/docs/content/integrations/keys.mdx

Rejection reason: Not a genuine path-echo per D1/skill, which define path-echo strictly as 'basename repeating a path SEGMENT'. Verified the folder contains keys.mdx (the keys integration OVERVIEW) plus keys-focus/keys-navigation/keys-usekey/keys-utilities/keys-patterns as sub-pages of that one integration; the prefix meaningfully groups sub-pages under the overview and disambiguates from a future second integration. The fix is churn/YAGNI: dropping the prefix yields generic focus.mdx/navigation.mdx that lose the keys-integration signal, and the promote-to-subfolder branch is explicitly conditioned on an anticipated-but-nonexistent second integration. Renaming churns meta.json ordering + internal links for thin docs overviews. Not a duplicate, but does not meet the bar.

### R-040 · tests · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/tsconfig.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/tsconfig.test.json, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/package.json
cli/server's 47 test files are excluded from the type-check gate, contradicting the AGENTS.md 'type-check covers source, test, AND build-script files' rule
Rejection reason: Factually false at the cited lines. The candidate claims 'cli/server/tsconfig.json line 27 excludes **/*.test.ts' and concludes the 47 test files 'get zero static type-checking in the gate'. The actual /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/cli/server/tsconfig.json is only 8 lines, extends ../../libs/core/tsconfig/node.json, has NO exclude field at all, and sets include:['src']. Because there is no test exclude and the test files live under src/ (47 of them, confirmed by rg), the bare `tsc --noEmit` type-check script DOES cover them: running `tsc --noEmit --listFiles` lists exactly all 47 cli/server src/**/*.test.ts files in the type-check program (verified: app.test.ts, http-server.test.ts, features/config/router.test.ts, etc.). The test files use explicit `import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest'` (e.g. src/shared/lib/paths.test.ts:4) rather than vitest/globals ambient types, so they type-check cleanly under node.json's types:['node']. The AGENTS.md rule 'type-check covers source, test, AND build-script files' is therefore SATISFIED by the single-pass config, not violated. The proposed fix (append `&& tsc --noEmit -p tsconfig.test.json`) would only re-check the same already-checked files — pure churn that fights context.md's intentional single-pass tsconfig topology ('Do NOT propose re-adding a *.test.* exclude'; there is no exclude to begin with). tsconfig.test.json is the vitest typecheck config, not evidence that tests are unchecked. Not a duplicate of F-144 (dead test:types scripts) or R-004 (cli/add + apps/docs/scripts), but rejected on factual grounds.
round: 5

### R-041 · dry · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/vite.config.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/vitest.config.ts

Rejection reason: Factually real but below the bar; fix is churn. apps/web/vite.config.ts:12 and vitest.config.ts:9 both declare the single line '@': path.resolve(__dirname,'./src'). That is a one-line config alias, not meaningful duplication. The vite/vitest split for web+landing is intentional per context.md. The proposed fix either merges the test block into vite.config.ts (undoing the intentional split) or makes vitest.config.ts import the alias object from vite.config.ts (import-coupling two config files to dedupe one line). Both churn more than the 1-line cost. Repo CLAUDE.md/sota-structure DRY guidance ('3 similar lines > unnecessary helper function', no premature abstraction) argues against flagging this. R-014 (apps/docs) was materially different: there the vite alias duplicated tsconfig paths while viteTsConfigPaths ALREADY resolved them (redundant work + a plugin doing it); here no plugin resolves the alias and the two configs are genuinely separate. Not a structural improvement.
round: 5

### R-042 · dry · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/apps/web/src/features/history/utils.tsx, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/core/src/review/history.ts
Web getRunSummary duplicates the passed/parts/Found-N branching of the shared getRunSummaryText
Rejection reason: Factually real at utils.tsx:17-36 and history.ts:68-75, and not a digest duplicate. But the fix is churn, not improvement. The web getRunSummary returns ReactNode and shares only two trivial string literals with getRunSummaryText ('Passed with no issues.' and the `Found N issue(s).` template); the substantive third branch renders JSX severity chips, wholly different from the helper's .join(', '). The proposed delegation would force getRunSummary to call getRunSummaryParts AND getRunSummaryText (the latter itself re-calls getRunSummaryParts), redundantly recomputing parts just to dedupe two one-line returns, and would make the passed/empty branches require cross-referencing a different module to understand. Per context.md ('extract ONLY on demonstrated reuse or a real readability cliff — never preemptively') and the skill's anti-fragmentation/locality rules, this trades a ~3-line local obviousness for a double-pipeline-call indirection. Cure worse than disease.
round: 5

### R-043 · architecture · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/keys/scripts/validate-registry-closure.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/registry/src/cli/bundler/index.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/ui/src/validation/registry-orphan-validator.ts, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/libs/keys/package.json
331-line registry import-closure validator hand-rolled in libs/keys/scripts instead of owned by libs/registry
Rejection reason: Factually the files exist as cited (libs/keys/scripts/validate-registry-closure.ts is a real 331-line module; libs/ui/src/validation/registry-import-validator.ts is a separate import-closure validator; libs/registry exports no equivalent). But this candidate is a recombination of already-handled digest findings plus a churny premature-abstraction recommendation. (1) Its core 'three packages hand-roll registry-closure logic' claim is inflated/inaccurate: scripts/monorepo/registry-closure.mjs (37 lines) walks the registryDependencies ITEM graph, a deliberately side-effect-free concern for the smoke test (its own header says so), NOT file import-closure; registry-orphan-validator.ts checks orphan files. Only TWO modules genuinely do import-closure, and they validate different registry shapes with library-specific policy (keys enforces src/hooks|core|dom path rules and per-item file inclusion; libs/ui's validateRegistryImportClosure does cross-item registryDependencies closure with @diffgazer/keys shim-satisfaction logic). They share machinery but diverge in policy. (2) The genuinely actionable duplication it cites is already covered: the RELATIVE_JS_IMPORT regex = F-082 (triplicated regex across keys scripts), the duplicated RegistryItem/RegistryFile types = F-083, and the libs/ui/src/validation misplacement = F-010 (misleading runtime-source shell holding build-time validators). (3) What remains uniquely is 'move closure logic into @diffgazer/registry as a generic validateRegistryImportClosure({registryPath,publicDir}) and re-point ui + scripts.mjs at it' — this would centralize divergent per-library policy behind a new parameterization layer, fighting the AGENTS.md/skill rule 'do not extract a helper only because two files look similar; extract when it names a real concept, removes meaningful duplication, and keeps call sites clearer.' Net: duplicate of F-010/F-082/F-083 on the real parts, and a fragmentation-fighting fix on the novel part. Evidence read in full: validate-registry-closure.ts:1-331, registry-import-validator.ts:1-90, registry-orphan-validator.ts:1-39, scripts/monorepo/registry-closure.mjs:1-37, libs/registry/src/index.ts:1-80.
round: 5

### R-044 · structure · /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/scripts/monorepo/artifacts/json.mjs, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/scripts/monorepo/artifacts/files.mjs, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/scripts/monorepo/artifacts/paths.mjs, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/scripts/monorepo/artifacts/env.mjs, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/scripts/monorepo/check-invariants.mjs, /Users/voitz/Projects/diffgazer-workspace/scripts/monorepo/benchmark-server.mjs
scripts/monorepo/artifacts/ is a mislabeled folder mixing generic infra helpers with artifact-domain logic
Rejection reason: Premise is factually inverted. The candidate claims scripts/monorepo/artifacts/ is 'mislabeled' because its generic helpers (json/files/paths/env) are the shared home for ALL monorepo scripts co-mingled with artifact logic. The actual import trace shows the dominant direction is the opposite: json.mjs/paths.mjs/files.mjs are consumed PRIMARILY by the artifact-domain modules inside the same folder (config.mjs:3-4, validation.mjs:4-6, sync.mjs:4-5 = 9 intra-folder import sites). Outside leakage is narrow: readJson is imported by only 2 external siblings (check-invariants.mjs:5, validate-artifacts.mjs:18) and BOTH are themselves artifact/invariant validators that also import ./artifacts/run-checks.mjs (the artifact orchestrator tail) — they belong to the artifact-validation family, not 'non-artifact' code. The only genuinely cross-cutting file is env.mjs (one 11-line env-var-name registry used by 6 smoke/benchmark scripts). The candidate's own fix is self-contradictory: it moves config.mjs to lib/, but config.mjs (parseDocsLibrariesConfig, assertSafeLibraryId, LIBRARY_ID_RE) is unambiguously artifact/docs-libraries domain config, not infra. A whole-folder split plus rewriting ./artifacts/* specifiers across ~8 files to relocate one shared file (env.mjs) and three artifact-internal node:fs/node:path wrappers is churn, not improvement, and fights the sota-structure anti-fragmentation bar (extract only on demonstrated reuse of a real named concept). context.md section 5 explicitly blesses 'root scripts/monorepo for orchestration ... all defensible.' A folder whose dominant content IS the artifact pipeline (sync, validation, config, pack-surface, benchmark-slo, run-checks) is reasonably named 'artifacts'. The folder's naming/colocation was already examined under F-074 and R-006; this adds a speculative reorganization without evidence the label is wrong. Real at cited lines but rejected as churn-not-improvement.
round: 5
